Passionate about IP! Since June 2003 the IPKat has covered copyright, patent, trade mark, designs, info-tech, privacy and confidentiality issues from a mainly UK and European perspective. <h2 class='title'>Not just any old IPKat ...</h2>
<div class='widget-content'>
<div><div style="text-align: justify;"><div style="font-weight: normal;">* "Most Popular Intellectual Property Law Blawg" of all time according to <a href="https://blawgsearch.justia.com/blogs/categories/intellectual-property-law?page=1&amp;sortby=popularity&amp;dispmode=list&amp;popmode=all"><b>Justia rankings</b></a>, November 2022.</div><div style="font-weight: normal;">* "Most Popular Copyright Blawg" of all time according to <a href="https://blawgsearch.justia.com/blogs/categories/copyright?page=1&amp;sortby=popularity&amp;dispmode=expanded&amp;popmode=all"><b>Justia rankings</b></a>, November 2022.<div><div style="text-align: justify;"><div style="font-weight: normal;">* PermaKat Eleonora Rosati received the  <a href="https://adepi.net/2022/07/14/eleonora-rosati-juan-molla-y-la-oei-premio-adepi-2022/"><b>2022 Adepi Award</b></a>.
</div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span =""  style="font-size:100%;">* PermaKat Eleonora Rosati listed as one of the World Intellectual Property Review's "Influential Women in IP" of 2020.</span></div><div style="font-weight: normal;"><span =""  style="font-size:100%;">* PermaKat Eleonora Rosati</span><span =""  style="font-size:100%;"> </span><span =""
